(function(fnUtils, CMP) {
const deferLoadTime = 5000;
const readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForThirdPartyTracking', { bubbles: true });
const readyForThirdPartyTracking = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForThirdPartyTracking'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForThirdPartyTrackingEvent);
});
const readyForDeferredScriptsEvent = new CustomEvent('readyForDeferredScripts', { bubbles: true });
const readyForDeferredScripts = fnUtils.once(function() {
window.dataLayer.push({event: 'readyForDeferredScripts'});
window.dispatchEvent(readyForDeferredScriptsEvent);
});
const hasTargetingConsentHandler = function() {
const hasConsent = CMP.hasTargetingConsent();
// Load GTM for consent-required countries when consent is granted
if (hasConsent && typeof window.loadGTMAfterConsent === 'function') {
window.loadGTMAfterConsent();
}
if (hasConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
// Trigger the readyForDeferredScripts if consent is given
// or if the user has closed the banner(AlertBox) which exists for EU
// or if the user optin consent is not required, which applies for non gdpr locations
if (hasConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed() || !CMP.isOptInConsent()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasConsent;
};
const purposeOneConsentHandler = async function() {
const hasPurposeOneConsent = await CMP.hasPurposeOneConsent();
// Load GTM for consent-required countries when consent is granted
if (hasPurposeOneConsent && typeof window.loadGTMAfterConsent === 'function') {
window.loadGTMAfterConsent();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
}
if (hasPurposeOneConsent || CMP.isAlertBoxClosed()) {
readyForDeferredScripts();
}
return hasPurposeOneConsent;
};
const onRequiredDomEvent = fnUtils.once(function() {
if (!CMP) {
readyForThirdPartyTracking();
readyForDeferredScripts();
return;
}
const handler = CMP.supportsTCData() ? purposeOneConsentHandler : hasTargetingConsentHandler;
if (!CMP.isLoading()) {
handler();
}
CMP.onConsentChange(handler);
});
[
['adRendered', onRequiredDomEvent],
['beforeunload', onRequiredDomEvent],
['load', function() { setTimeout(onRequiredDomEvent, deferLoadTime); }]
].forEach(function(event) {
window.addEventListener(event[0], event[1], { once: true });
});

<div id="heading_1-0" class="comp heading heading--updated-article-header"> <h1 class="heading__title">Banana Bread</h1>
<p class="heading__subtitle">Put those ripe bananas to use in this moist, delicious banana bread and you'll learn why it's the most popular recipe on Simply Recipes.</p>
</div>
<div id="article-meta_1-0" class="comp article-meta mntl-article-meta mntl-block article-meta--updated-article-header has-image attribution-enabled single-author" data-tracking-container="true"><div id="bylines_1-0" class="comp bylines lifestyle-food-bylines mntl-bylines"><div id="mntl-bylines__group_1-0" class="comp mntl-bylines__group mntl-block mntl-bylines__group--author"><div id="mntl-bylines__item_1-0" class="comp mntl-bylines__item mntl-attribution__item mntl-attribution__item--has-date">

alt="Elise Bauer"
/>
</noscript></div>

<div id="jump-btn-wrapper_1-0" class="comp jump-btn-wrapper mntl-block"><button id="recipe-jump-button_1-0" class="comp recipe-jump-button mntl-button text-label-300 button--contained-standard"> Jump to recipe
<svg class="icon icon-arrow-down mntl-button__icon "
>
<use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="#icon-arrow-down" href="#icon-arrow-down"></use>
</svg>
</button></div>
<div id="article__header--project_1-0" class="comp article__header--project mntl-sc-page mntl-block article-intro text-passage structured-content" data-sc-sticky-offset="235" data-sc-ad-label-height="11" data-sc-ad-track-spacing="100" data-sc-min-track-height="250" data-sc-max-track-height="600" data-sc-breakpoint="50em" data-sc-load-immediate="1" data-sc-content-positions="[1, 1, 1, 1, 1, 1, 1]" data-bind-scroll-on-start="true"><p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> This banana bread has been the most popular recipe on Simply Recipes for over 10 years. Thousands of people make it every day. Why?
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_2-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_3-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Because it really is the best banana bread recipe, period. You can mix everything in one bowl, you can vary the amount of sugar or bananas. And the secret to its great flavor? <strong>Melted butter.<span class="ql-cursor"></span></strong>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_4-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_5-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image--no-theme no-theme figure-landscape figure-high-res"> <div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:66.6%;">
<img

</noscript>
</div> </div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0" class="comp mntl-figure-caption text-utility-100 figure-article-caption"> <span class="figure-article-caption-owner">Kelly Hamilton</span>
</figcaption></figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_6-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> The beauty of this banana bread recipe is you don&#39;t need a fancy mixer! A mixing bowl, a fork to whisk the eggs, and a sturdy spoon to mix the batter are all you need. The sugar amount is flexible. The original recipe called for a cup of white sugar, but most people, including me, do just fine with 3/4 cup, and many are happy with 1/2 cup.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_7-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_8-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> You can toss in a cup of chopped nuts, raisins, or chocolate chips if you want, or put the batter into muffin tins and make <a href="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/recipes/banana_nut_muffins/" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">banana nut muffins</a> instead. You can even go a step further and make <a href="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/recipes/chocolate_banana_bread/" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="2">chocolate banana bread</a>.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_9-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_10-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image--no-theme no-theme figure-landscape figure-high-res"> <div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:66.6%;">
<img
data-src="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/thmb/L4nBpdZCubnbGtVbOW90JQSBVWc=/1500x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/Simply-Recipes-Easy-Banana-Bread-LEAD-2-2-63dd39af009945d58f5bf4c2ae8d6070.jpg"

</div> </div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_2-0" class="comp mntl-figure-caption text-utility-100 figure-article-caption"> <span class="figure-article-caption-owner">Kelly Hamilton</span>
</figcaption></figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_11-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> I was given this banana bread recipe years ago from my friend Heidi H, who, many years before, had begged the recipe from a ski buddy’s mother—Mrs. Hockmeyer. Thanks Heidi!
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_12-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_13-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-callout mntl-sc-block-callout mntl-block theme-fastfacts text-passage" data-tracking-id="mntl-sc-block-callout" data-tracking-container="true"><h3 id="mntl-sc-block-callout-heading_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-callout-heading mntl-text-block">The Backstory on the #1 Banana Bread Recipe</h3>
<div id="mntl-sc-block-callout-body_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-callout-body mntl-text-block text-passage"><p>All these years later, we were curious to know more about who Mrs. Hockmeyer is, and how Heidi got her recipe in the first place. <a href="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/the-internets-most-popular-banana-bread-recipe-7377365" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">You can read all about it in this story.</a></p></div></div></div>
<div id="structured-project-content_1-0" class="comp structured-project-content mntl-block article__content right-rail structured-content"><div id="recipe-editorial-block_1-0" class="comp recipe-editorial-block mntl-sc-page mntl-block text-passage" data-sc-sticky-offset="60" data-sc-ad-label-height="24" data-sc-ad-track-spacing="100" data-sc-min-track-height="250" data-sc-max-track-height="600" data-sc-breakpoint="50em" data-sc-load-immediate="1" data-sc-content-positions="[300,600,900,1200,1500,1800,2100]" data-bind-scroll-on-start="true"><span class="heading-toc" id="toc-the-best-loaf-pan-for-this-recipe"></span><h2 id="mntl-sc-block_14-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text text-title-300"> The Best Loaf Pan for This Recipe </span> </h2>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_15-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> This recipe calls for an 8x4-inch loaf pan, which produces a tall loaf. The recipe will also work in an 8 1/2x4 1/2-inch loaf pan, producing a slightly shorter bread. Since the pan is a bit larger, the bake time is shorter: 47 to 57 minutes. A 9x5-inch pan will yield an especially short but still delicious bread; bake for 45 to 55 minutes.
</p>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-how-our-readers-adapt-this-banana-bread-recipe"></span><h2 id="mntl-sc-block_16-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text text-title-300"> How Our Readers Adapt This Banana Bread Recipe </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_17-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> <li>Natalie: &#34;I added a drizzle of maple syrup on top, plus some blueberries. I also switched out the flour for 1 cup of almond meal and 1 cup of gluten-free flour.&#34;</li><li>Roberta: &#34;Added mini chocolate chips in batter and topped with crumb topping. Excellent!&#34;</li><li>Eleanor: &#34;I was out of eggs, so I substituted with a flax egg and it turned out perfectly! A tablespoon of flaxseed with 2 1/2 tablespoons of water and let rest for 5-10 minutes in place of the egg.&#34;</li><li>Monica: &#34;The BEST banana bread recipe there is. I sprinkle demerara sugar on top before baking and it gives it a delicious crunch!&#34;</li><li>Lisa: &#34;I’ve been making this loaf for years. I always add a tablespoon or two of molasses, which gives a punchier flavor and darker color. I make it with chocolate chips for the kids and with cranberries and pecans for the adults.&#34;</li><li>LeRoy: &#34;My wife, Mary created &#34;Elvis Bread&#34; and added half a bag of Reese&#39;s Peanut Butter Chips.&#34;</li><li>Marione: &#34;THE BEST banana bread I’ve made. I added pineapple tidbits and substituted part of white sugar with brown sugar.&#34;<br/></li>
</ul>

</ul>

<h2 id="recipe-block__header_1-0" class="comp recipe-block__header text-block"> Banana Bread
</h2>
<div id="recipe-block__meta_1-0" class="comp recipe-block__meta mntl-block"><div id="project-meta_1-0" class="comp project-meta">
<div class="project-meta__times-container">
<div class="prep-time project-meta__prep-time">
<span class="meta-text">
<span class="meta-text__label">Prep Time</span>
<span class="meta-text__data">10 mins</span>
</span>
</div>
<div class="cook-time project-meta__cook-time">
<span class="meta-text">
<span class="meta-text__label">Cook Time</span>
<span class="meta-text__data">60 mins</span>
</span>
</div>
<div class="total-time project-meta__total-time">
<span class="meta-text">
<span class="meta-text__label">Total Time</span>
<span class="meta-text__data">70 mins</span>
</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="project-meta__results-container">
<div class="recipe-serving project-meta__recipe-serving">
<span class="meta-text">
<span class="meta-text__label">Servings</span>
<span class="meta-text__data">8
to 10 servings</span>
</span>
</div>
<div class="recipe-yield project-meta__recipe-yield">
<span class="meta-text">
<span class="meta-text__label">Yield</span>
<span class="meta-text__data">1 loaf</span>
</span>
</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<div id="recipe-block__note_1-0" class="comp recipe-block__note mntl-block text-passage"><div id="recipe-block__note-text_1-0" class="comp recipe-block__note-text text-block"> <p>No need for a mixer for this recipe! Clean-up is easy, too. If you want, you can mix everything in one bowl.<br/></p><p>This recipe calls for an 8x4-inch loaf pan. If you are baking in an 8 1/2x4 1/2-inch pan, bake for 47 to 57 minutes. If baking in a 9x5-inch pan, bake for 45 to 55 minutes. Note that the larger pan size will produce a flatter loaf.</p><p>The best bananas to use for banana bread are those that are overripe. The yellow peels should be at least half browned, and the bananas inside squishy and browning.</p>
</div></div></div>
<div id="mm-recipes-screen-wake_1-0" class="comp mm-recipes-screen-wake" data-screen-wake-locked="false"> <button
id="mm-recipes-screen-wake__button-1-0"

aria-pressed="false"
aria-label="Toggle Screen Wake"
data-tracking-container="true"
data-tracking-category="User Recipe Action"
data-tracking-subcategory="Screen Wake"
data-tracking-subtype="On"
>
<span class="mm-recipes-screen-wake__slider"></span>
</button>
<span class="mm-recipes-screen-wake__label">
Keep Screen Awake
</span>
</div>
<section id="section--ingredients_1-0" class="comp section--ingredients section"> <header class="section__header "><h3 class="section__title section__title--bold-underline" data-title-tag="">Ingredients</h3></header>
<div class="loc section-content section__content "><div id="structured-ingredients_1-0" class="comp structured-ingredients">
<ul class="structured-ingredients__list text-passage">
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">2 to 3</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">medium (7&#34; to 7-7/8&#34; long)</span> <a href="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/how-to-freeze-bananas-5197263" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1"><span data-ingredient-name="true">very ripe bananas</span></a><span data-ingredient-name="true">, peeled (about 1 1/4 to 1 1/2 cups mashed)</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1/3</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup (76g)</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">butter, unsalted or salted, melted</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1/2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">teaspoon</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">baking soda (not baking powder)</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">pinch</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">salt</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">3/4</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cup</span> (150g) <span data-ingredient-name="true">sugar (1/2 cup if you would like it less sweet, 1 cup if more sweet)</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">large</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">egg, beaten</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">teaspoon</span> <span data-ingredient-name="true">vanilla extract</span></p>
</li>
<li class="structured-ingredients__list-item">
<p><span data-ingredient-quantity="true">1 1/2</span> <span data-ingredient-unit="true">cups</span> (205g) <span data-ingredient-name="true">all-purpose flour</span></p>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<div id="mm-ads-native_1-0" class="comp mm-ads-native mm-ads-native--labeled" style="--native-ad-height: auto"><div id="mm-ads-native__adunit_1-0" class="comp mm-ads-native__adunit mm-ads-gpt-dynamic-adunit mm-ads-gpt-adunit gpt native dynamic">
<div id="native" class="wrapper"
data-type="native" data-pos="native" data-priority="4" data-sizes="[[1, 3],&quot;fluid&quot;]" data-rtb="false" data-wait-for-third-party="false" data-targeting="{}"></div>
</div></div>
<section id="section--instructions_1-0" class="comp section--instructions section"> <header class="section__header "><h3 class="section__title section__title--bold-underline" data-title-tag="">Method</h3></header>
<div class="loc section-content section__content "><div id="structured-project__steps_1-0" class="comp structured-project__steps mntl-sc-page mntl-block text-passage structured-content" data-sc-sticky-offset="60" data-sc-ad-label-height="24" data-sc-ad-track-spacing="100" data-sc-min-track-height="250" data-sc-max-track-height="600" data-sc-breakpoint="50em" data-sc-load-immediate="1" data-sc-content-positions="[300,600,900,1200,1500,1800,2100]" data-bind-scroll-on-start="true"><OL id="mntl-sc-block_21-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--OL">
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_22-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<div id="mntl-sc-block_23-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-subheading mntl-sc-block-subheading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-subheading__text"> Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C): </span> </div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_24-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Butter an 8x4-inch loaf pan.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_25-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_27-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<div id="mntl-sc-block_28-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-subheading mntl-sc-block-subheading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-subheading__text"> Mash the bananas and add the butter: </span> </div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_29-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> In a mixing bowl, mash the ripe bananas with a fork until completely smooth. Stir the melted butter into the mashed bananas.
</p>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_30-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image--no-theme no-theme figure-landscape figure-high-res"> <div class="figure-media">

<div id="mntl-sc-block_32-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_34-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<div id="mntl-sc-block_35-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-subheading mntl-sc-block-subheading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-subheading__text"> Mix in the remaining ingredients: </span> </div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_36-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Mix in the baking soda and salt. Stir in the sugar, beaten egg, and vanilla extract. Mix in the flour.
</p>

<div id="mntl-sc-block_42-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-subheading mntl-sc-block-subheading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-subheading__text"> Bake the bread: </span> </div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_43-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Pour the batter into your prepared loaf pan.
</p>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_44-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image--no-theme no-theme figure-landscape figure-high-res"> <div class="figure-media">

data-sizes="750px"

class="lazyload mntl-image mntl-image universal-image__image"
data-expand="300"
data-hi-res-src="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/thmb/oLck4cCTWrp9ofK2U1lliksSUL8=/1500x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/Simply-Recipes-Easy-Banana-Bread-METHOD-5-a9a9c4e47f7a46e2adbf3b423606604a.jpg"
id=mntl-sc-block-image_7-0
data-tracking-container="true"
data-img-lightbox="true"
data-click-tracked="true"
/>
<noscript>
<img
src="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/thmb/oLck4cCTWrp9ofK2U1lliksSUL8=/1500x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/Simply-Recipes-Easy-Banana-Bread-METHOD-5-a9a9c4e47f7a46e2adbf3b423606604a.jpg"
width="5184"
height="3456"
class="img--noscript mntl-image mntl-image universal-image__image"
srcset="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/thmb/7P4CVOCZO0Y8Erfn3f0kRMMz6Nk=/750x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/Simply-Recipes-Easy-Banana-Bread-METHOD-5-a9a9c4e47f7a46e2adbf3b423606604a.jpg 750w"
sizes="750px"
alt="Banana bread batter poured into a loaf pan."
/>
</noscript>
</div> </div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_7-0" class="comp mntl-figure-caption text-utility-100 figure-article-caption"> <span class="figure-article-caption-owner">Kelly Hamilton</span>
</figcaption></figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_45-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Bake for 55 to 65 minutes at 350°F (175°C), or until a toothpick or wooden skewer inserted into the center comes out clean. A few dry crumbs are okay; streaks of wet batter are not. If the outside of the loaf is browned but the center is still wet, loosely tent the loaf with foil and continue baking until the loaf is fully baked.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_46-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
</LI>
<LI id="mntl-sc-block_48-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-startgroup mntl-sc-block-group--LI">
<div id="mntl-sc-block_49-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-subheading mntl-sc-block-subheading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-subheading__text"> Cool and serve: </span> </div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_50-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Remove from oven and let cool in the pan for a few minutes. Then remove the banana bread from the pan and let cool completely before serving. Slice and serve. (A bread knife helps to make slices that aren&#39;t crumbly.)
</p>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_51-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-html"> Wrapped well, the&nbsp;banana&nbsp;bread&nbsp;will keep at room temperature for 4 days. For longer storage, refrigerate the loaf up to 5 days, or <a href="https://www.simplyrecipes.com/how_to_store_and_freeze_banana_bread/" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">freeze it</a>.
</p>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_52-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block lifestyle-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-image--no-theme no-theme figure-landscape figure-high-res"> <div class="figure-media">

<span class="card__title">
<span class="card__underline">
Lemon Rosemary Zucchini Bread
</span>
</span>
</div>
<div class="loc card__footer"><span id="meta-text--recipe_1-0" class="comp meta-text--recipe meta-text">
<svg class="meta-text__icon">
<use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="#icon-clock"></use>
</svg>
<span class="meta-text__text">
60 mins

function overwriteIframeTitle(mutationList, embedTitle, observer) {
for (const mutation of mutationList) {
if (mutation.type === 'childList') {
const parentNode = mutationList[0].target;
// Grab iframe from parentNode
const iframe = parentNode.querySelector('iframe');
if (iframe !== null) {
// Overwrite iframe title attr with title from Selene
iframe.title = embedTitle;
observer.disconnect();
// Early return, prevent further looping for other mutations
return;
}
}
}
}
function observeChildNodeChanges(embed) {
const config = {
childList: true,
subtree: true
};
/* Explicitly use arrow function for the callback executed on
observed node to pass in embed title to overwrite iframe title */
const observer = new MutationObserver((mutationList) => {
overwriteIframeTitle(mutationList, embed.dataset.title, observer);
});
observer.observe(embed, config);
}
function observerCallback(entries, observer) {
entries.forEach((entry) => {

const digiohEmbed = entry.target;
if (Mntl.digioh.initialized) {
observer.unobserve(digiohEmbed);
} else {
Mntl.digioh.types.load(() => observer.unobserve(digiohEmbed));
}
}
});

observer.observe(embed);

});
}
